勢力図は日毎に変動し、精確な把握は誰にも不可能という状況にまで陥っている。　ただ渡島半島を制圧し、本国との補給線を確立した露帝軍の優越は誰の目にも瞭然であった。
The chart of power fluctuated day by day, and it was impossible for anyone to have a precise grasp of the situation.　However, the superiority of the Russian Imperial Army, which had conquered the Toshima Peninsula and established a supply line with the home country, was obvious to all.

時間の長短はさて置き、やがて露帝は北曾の支配を完了し、本州侵攻に取り掛かるだろうと見られていた。　　だが――――

傭兵帝国。聖堂 craft士団。軍隊派遣会社……　通称〝武帝〟。
Mercenary Empire. Sanctuary crafters group. Military dispatch club ...... Commonly known as "Wudi".

その集団は北曾西南、渡島半島から西へ海を隔てて五〇キロ程の、松前大島を根城とする。　海産物の豊富な環境であるが、彼らは漁業に関心を示すことがなかった。
The group is based on Matsumae Oshima Island, about 50 kilometers west of the Watashima Peninsula in the southwest of Hokuso.　Although the island is rich in marine products, they have never shown any interest in fishing.

彼らの生業は戦争である。
Their livelihood is war.

近隣を切り従え、領土を広げようとするのではない。　そうした侵略を望む者に、又はその侵略を防ごうとする者に、雇われて戦うのだ。
We do not seek to cut off our neighbors and expand our territory.　We are hired to fight those who want to invade or prevent such invasion.

彼らは理非を問わない。国家を問わず民族を問わず宗教も主義主張も一切問わない。　契約条件が満たされるか否か。雇用の諾否を決するのはその一事のみである。
They do not question reason or principle. They don't care about nations, ethnicities, religions, or principles.　The only thing that determines whether or not a contract is fulfilled is whether or not the terms of the contract are met. That is the only thing that decides whether or not to accept employment.

条件はやや、特殊なものであったが。　金銭面から見る限り、彼らが雇用者へ提供する戦力は値に対して全く破格と云えたろう。
The conditions were somewhat unique.　As far as money is concerned, the strength they provide to their employers is absolutely unparalleled in relation to the value.

〝武帝〟の戦闘力の中心は、真打 tsurugiを有する mushaが担う。
The core of the fighting force of the "Warrior Emperor" is musha, who possesses the "true strike" tsurugi.

高速徹甲弾、発振砲等、対竜 craft兵用狙撃兵器の発達に伴って数打 tsurugiと真打 tsurugiの力関係は劇的な逆転を遂げた。　最新の兵器は、真打の古い統御機能では扱えない。
With the development of high speed armor-piercing bombs, oscillating cannons, and other sniper weapons for use against dragon craft soldiers, the power relationship between several tsurugi and shinpachi has been dramatically reversed.　The latest weapons could not be handled by the old control functions of the true strike.

白兵戦を表芸とする真打 mushaにとって、栄光は過去のものとなった。　数打 tsurugiを雑器、安物、紛い物と、嗤っていられた時代は永遠に過ぎ去ったのだ。
The glory of Shin'uchi musha, whose main art is white-knuckle fighting, has become a thing of the past.　The days when we could laugh at tsurugi as a miscellaneous weapon, a cheap product, or an imitation are gone forever.

それでも彼らの多くは craft士階級、つまり前線で戦うよりも指揮統率を任務とする者であったから、軍隊に居場所を全く失ったわけではない。　最強の実戦力とは見做されなくなっただけである。
Still, many of them were of the craft class, those who were tasked with command and control rather than fighting on the front lines, so they did not lose their place in the army at all.　It's just that they are no longer regarded as the strongest actual fighting force.

しかし、最強戦力たる自負こそは彼らの軍指揮権に、延いては階級意識に正当性を与える根拠であったため、数打 mushaの台頭に耐えられず、逃げるように軍籍から離れた者は少なくなかった。
However, since the pride of being the strongest force was the basis for giving legitimacy to their military command and eventually to their class consciousness, many of them could not withstand the rise of the Musha and left the military as if to escape.

そんな逸れ mushaを〝武帝〟は受け入れ……　そして、彼らに自己認識を取り戻させた。
The "warrior emperor" accepted such deviant musha ...... and made them regain their self-awareness.

正面戦闘の優位を数打に譲ろうと、真打 mushaは未だ強猛な存在には違いない。　彼らの多くは高い性能、熟練の技術、豊富な経験を兼ね備える。
Even if they give up their head-to-head combat advantage to a few hits, the true musha are still a formidable force to be reckoned with.　Many of them combine high performance, skill, and a wealth of experience.

一 craftで重戦車の隊列を相手取り、砲兵陣地を砕くも困難としない。　いや最新の竜 craft兵さえ、状況と戦術を選んで格闘戦に持ち込めば互角以上に戦える――むしろ圧倒できる。
A single craft can take on a column of heavy tanks and shatter artillery positions with no difficulty.　No, even the latest dragon craft soldiers are more than capable of fighting on even terms if they choose the right situation and tactics to engage in combat - in fact, they can overwhelm you.

運用の仕方を誤らねば、多大な戦果を挙げ得るのだ。　　つまり〝武帝〟はそうして、両者の要望に応えた。誇りを求める mushaと、力を求める依頼者の。
If it is not used in the wrong way, it can be very effective.　　In other words, this is how the Warrior Emperor responded to the needs of both parties. The musha for pride, and the client for power.

俄かに出現した孤島の傭兵団が短時日で名を成した所以はここにある。
This is the reason why a group of isolated island mercenaries suddenly appeared and made a name for themselves in a short time.

広く知られてゆくにつれ、〝武帝〟への依頼は数を増やした――その陰惨な契約条件にも関わらず。　大和で、大陸で、あるいは更に遠方で。彼らは頼まれるまま数多の戦闘に加わり、勝利と死を積み重ねた。
As the word got out, the number of requests to the "Warrior Emperor" increased - despite the gruesome terms of the contract.　In Yamato, on the continent, or even farther afield. They took part in as many battles as they were asked to, accumulating victories and deaths.

大和や露帝がこの剣呑な不法占拠者を松前大島から追い出そうと兵を繰り出すこともあったが……　その試みは毎回、あたかも重力の働きが狂ったかのような異様な嵐に阻まれ、頓挫している。
The Yamato and Russian emperors sometimes sent troops to remove these swashbuckling squatters from Matsumae Oshima. ...... Each attempt was thwarted by a strange storm, as if gravity had gone awry.

海上交通を妨げる意図が見えないこともあり、昨今は両国も〝武帝〟の存在を消極的に承認しつつあった。　非公式には――時として積極的に利用することさえも。
With no apparent intention to hinder maritime traffic, both countries have recently begun to reluctantly acknowledge the existence of the "Warrior Emperor".　Unofficially - and sometimes even actively - they use it.

かくして傭兵帝国は極東に立つ。　混沌窮まる情勢の渦中を縦横無尽に駆け巡り、戦い、殺し――そうする中で更に武威を高め、存在感を高め、名の持つ圧力を高めながら。
Thus, the mercenary empire stands in the Far East.　In the midst of the chaos and confusion of the situation, they run around, fight, and kill - while further increasing their military prowess, presence, and the pressure of their name.

頼り縋る者を日毎に増やしながら。　忌み嫌う者をも、同じ速さで増やしながら。
Day by day, the number of people we rely on and cling to grows.　The number of people who hate us is increasing at the same rate.
